        <p class="leading-relaxed">Integrate nationality prediction directly into your workflows and perform efficient inference on big datasets with our simple APIs built for high volumes. Get started quickly with community libraries for any programming language.</p>

    <div class="bg-stone-400/10 p-4 rounded-md">
        <span class="hero-code-bracket-square h-7 w-7 mb-8"></span>
        <h3 class="text-sm font-bold font-mono mb-2">Full Name Parsing</h3>
        <p class="text-sm">Our name parsing algorithm allows you to pass full names to our API's.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="bg-stone-400/10 p-4 rounded-md">
        <span class="hero-language h-7 w-7 mb-8"></span>
        <h3 class="text-sm font-bold font-mono mb-2">Diacritics and Accents</h3>
        <p class="text-sm">We support diacritics from any language as well as non-latin alphabets.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="bg-stone-400/10 p-4 rounded-md">
        <span class="hero-globe-alt h-7 w-7 mb-8"></span>
        <h3 class="text-sm font-bold font-mono mb-2">Localization</h3>
        <p class="text-sm"><a href="/our-data" class="font-inherit decoration-1 underline-offset-2 text-sky-600 underline hover:text-sky-700">Our dataset</a> covers the whole planet and we support scoping your requests to specific countries.</p>

        <h2 class="text-3xl font-bold font-mono mb-4">Upload and Process CSV Files</h2>
        <p class="leading-relaxed mb-4">Looking to enrich your data with demographic insights? Our CSV tool allows you to upload your data and have <b>gender</b>, <b>age</b> and <b>nationality</b> added in minutes.</p>
        <p class="leading-relaxed">Using CSV processing is a quick way to gain insights into your users, audience, prospects and customers by analysing their demographic composition.</p>

          <h2 class="text-3xl font-bold font-mono text-center mx-auto mb-12">Frequently Asked Questions</h2>
<div itemscope itemtype="https://schema.org/FAQPage">
    <ul>
        <li itemscope itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question" class="border-b-1 border-stone-400/50 pb-4 mb-4 cursor-pointer" phx-click="[[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-#i{i}&quot;}],[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-open-0&quot;}],[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-close-0&quot;}]]">
            <div class="flex flex-row gap-8">
                <h3 itemprop="name" class="font-mono font-bold grow justify-center">How can you tell if a name is male or female?</h3>
                <button>
                    <span id="faq-open-0" class="hero-plus "></span>
                    <span id="faq-close-0" class="hero-minus hidden"></span>
                </button>
            </div>
            <div id="faq-0" itemscope itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer" class="pr-12 data-[active=false]:hidden mt-4" data-active="false">
                <p itemprop="text" class="leading-relaxed">Most names are predominantly used for either males or females, so a statistical approach will often yield good results. Of course, some names are used across both sexes, but a statistical approach will reveal that, too. Furthermore, naming conventions can rely on cultural differences. We cover that with support for scoping a lookup to a specific country.</p>
            </div>
        </li><li itemscope itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question" class="border-b-1 border-stone-400/50 pb-4 mb-4 cursor-pointer" phx-click="[[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-#i{i}&quot;}],[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-open-1&quot;}],[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-close-1&quot;}]]">
            <div class="flex flex-row gap-8">
                <h3 itemprop="name" class="font-mono font-bold grow justify-center">How accurate is the tool in determining gender from names and how does it handle unisex names?</h3>
                <button>
                    <span id="faq-open-1" class="hero-plus "></span>
                    <span id="faq-close-1" class="hero-minus hidden"></span>
                </button>
            </div>
            <div id="faq-1" itemscope itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer" class="pr-12 data-[active=false]:hidden mt-4" data-active="false">
                <p itemprop="text" class="leading-relaxed">Our predictions are based on the ratio of males to females with a given name. As such, the accuracy is based on whether a name is strictly used by one gender or as a unisex name. We return a probability with all predictions. A probability closing towards 50% means that both genders use the name with equal likelihood.</p>
            </div>
        </li><li itemscope itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question" class="border-b-1 border-stone-400/50 pb-4 mb-4 cursor-pointer" phx-click="[[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-#i{i}&quot;}],[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-open-2&quot;}],[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-close-2&quot;}]]">
            <div class="flex flex-row gap-8">
                <h3 itemprop="name" class="font-mono font-bold grow justify-center">How does the tool handle names from different cultural or ethnic backgrounds?</h3>
                <button>
                    <span id="faq-open-2" class="hero-plus "></span>
                    <span id="faq-close-2" class="hero-minus hidden"></span>
                </button>
            </div>
            <div id="faq-2" itemscope itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer" class="pr-12 data-[active=false]:hidden mt-4" data-active="false">
                <p itemprop="text" class="leading-relaxed">Naming conventions can be different across countries and cultures. We support scoping a classification to a specific country which will often improve the accuracy of your results.</p>
            </div>
        </li><li itemscope itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question" class="border-b-1 border-stone-400/50 pb-4 mb-4 cursor-pointer" phx-click="[[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-#i{i}&quot;}],[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-open-3&quot;}],[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-close-3&quot;}]]">
            <div class="flex flex-row gap-8">
                <h3 itemprop="name" class="font-mono font-bold grow justify-center">Do you offer any free plans?</h3>
                <button>
                    <span id="faq-open-3" class="hero-plus "></span>
                    <span id="faq-close-3" class="hero-minus hidden"></span>
                </button>
            </div>
            <div id="faq-3" itemscope itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer" class="pr-12 data-[active=false]:hidden mt-4" data-active="false">
                <p itemprop="text" class="leading-relaxed">We do - and you won&#39;t even have to sign up. You can process 100 names/day with our API or CSV tool and we&#39;ll limit you based on your IP.</p>
            </div>
        </li><li itemscope itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question" class="border-b-1 border-stone-400/50 pb-4 mb-4 cursor-pointer" phx-click="[[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-#i{i}&quot;}],[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-open-4&quot;}],[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-close-4&quot;}]]">
            <div class="flex flex-row gap-8">
                <h3 itemprop="name" class="font-mono font-bold grow justify-center">Can the tool be integrated with our customer relationship management (CRM) systems?</h3>
                <button>
                    <span id="faq-open-4" class="hero-plus "></span>
                    <span id="faq-close-4" class="hero-minus hidden"></span>
                </button>
            </div>
            <div id="faq-4" itemscope itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer" class="pr-12 data-[active=false]:hidden mt-4" data-active="false">
                <p itemprop="text" class="leading-relaxed">There&#39;s plenty of ways to start integrating our prediction services with your existing tools. The easiest way to get started is with our no-code, official Zapier app.</p>
            </div>
        </li><li itemscope itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question" class="border-b-1 border-stone-400/50 pb-4 mb-4 cursor-pointer" phx-click="[[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-#i{i}&quot;}],[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-open-5&quot;}],[&quot;toggle&quot;,{&quot;to&quot;:&quot;#faq-close-5&quot;}]]">
            <div class="flex flex-row gap-8">
                <h3 itemprop="name" class="font-mono font-bold grow justify-center">What kind of customer support do you offer?</h3>
                <button>
                    <span id="faq-open-5" class="hero-plus "></span>
                    <span id="faq-close-5" class="hero-minus hidden"></span>
                </button>
            </div>
            <div id="faq-5" itemscope itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer" class="pr-12 data-[active=false]:hidden mt-4" data-active="false">
                <p itemprop="text" class="leading-relaxed">We&#39;re available on email to answer questions and help you out in integrating gender classification as part of your workflow. Reach out at info@genderize.io.</p>
